                                   16282             +*/*                                                              @L5C*/
                                   16283             +*/*01* FUNCTION = The Job Management routines construct a JFCB       */
                                   16284             +*/*         for each ddname specified in a job step.  In a           */
                                   16285             +*/*         concatenated data set, each of the multiple DD cards     */
                                   16286             +*/*         is given a ddname of blanks.  A JFCB is then             */
                                   16287             +*/*         concatenated for each DD, including those with a name    */
                                   16288             +*/*         of blanks.  It is brought into virtual storage when      */
                                   16289             +*/*         the data set is opened.  Information in a JFCB may be    */
                                   16290             +*/*         modified during OPEN processing.                         */
                                   16291             +*/*                                                                  */

0                                  16440             +*/*      For both PL/S and assembler, the following macro        @01A*/
                                   16441             +*/*      variables are defined for use in determining the        @01A*/
                                   16442             +*/*      current version of the JFCB at assemble / compile       @01A*/
                                   16443             +*/*      time:                                                   @01A*/
                                   16444             +*/*                                                                  */
                                   16445             +*/*      JFCB_FLD_VERSION  - Set to one of the following values  @01A*/
                                   16446             +*/*                          to indicate the current version     @01A*/
                                   16447             +*/*      JFCBTDSI_DEFINED  - The JFCBTDSI field exists at this   @01A*/
                                   16448             +*/*                          version of the macro                @01A*/
                                   16449             +*/*                                                                  */
                                   16450             +*/*      Additional variables will be defined here as            @01A*/
                                   16451             +*/*      incompatible changes are made to this macro.            @01A*/
                                   16452             +*/*                                                                  */
                                   16453             +*/*      These variables are defined in this macro beginning     @01A*/
                                   16454             +*/*      with HBB4420 and HBB4430 with OY59716 applied.  At all  @01A*/
                                   16455             +*/*      lower levels of this macro, these variables will have   @01A*/
                                   16456             +*/*      a zero value.                                           @01A*/
                                   16457             +*/*                                                                  */
                                   16458             +*/*      Usage example:                                          @01A*/
                                   16459             +*/*                                                                  */
                                   16460             +*/*        The following code defines the JFCBTDSI field only    @01A*/
                                   16461             +*/*        if it is not already defined in the level of IEFJFCBN @01A*/
                                   16462             +*/*        being used for the compile (semi-colons deliberately  @01A*/
                                   16463             +*/*        omitted).  Assembler usage is similar.                @01A*/
                                   16464             +*/*------------------------------------------------------------------*/
                                   16465             +*/*        %IF JFCB_FLD_VERSION > 0 %THEN                        @01A*/
                                   16466             +*/*          %GOTO TDSI1                                         @01A*/
                                   16467             +*/*        %ELSE                                                 @01A*/
                                   16468             +*/*          %                                                   @01A*/
                                   16469             +*/*                                                                  */
                                   16470             +*/*        DCL JFCBTDSI BIT(16) DEF(JFCVINDX)                    @01A*/
                                   16471             +*/*        %TDSI1:                                               @01A*/
                                   16472             +*/*------------------------------------------------------------------*/
                                   16473             +*/*        The IF test could be written                          @01A*/
                                   16474             +*/*                                                                  */
                                   16475             +*/*        %IF JFCB_FLD_VERSION >= 1 %THEN                       @01A*/
                                   16476             +*/*                                                                  */
                                   16477             +*/*        The preceding tests will work at any level of         @01A*/
                                   16478             +*/*        IEFJFCBN, even if the macro version does not          @01A*/
                                   16479             +*/*        define JFCB_FLD_VERSION (since it will default to     @01A*/
                                   16480             +*/*        zero if not defined).                                 @01A*/
                                   16481             +*/*                                                                  */
                                   16482             +*/*        If it is known that the including source code will    @01A*/
                                   16483             +*/*        always be compiled against a version of IEFJFCBN      @01A*/
                                   16484             +*/*        that has the macro variables defined, the IF test can @01A*/
                                   16485             +*/*        use the macro variable name that represents the       @01A*/
                                   16486             +*/*        desired level of the macro:                           @01A*/
                                   16487             +*/*                                                                  */
                                   16488             +*/*        %IF JFCB_FLD_VERSION >= JFCBTDSI_DEFINED %THEN        @01A*/
                                   16489             +*/*                                                                  */
                                   16490             +*/********************************************************************/

                                   16611             +*/*     than bit values.                                         @L7A*/

                                   16613             +*/*     FIXED(15) to FIXED(16).  The JFCBABST was declared as    @P3A*/
                                   16614             +*/*     a Halfword in the Assembler version, and should be able  @P3A*/
                                   16615             +*/*     to store value up to 64K.  However, declaring it as a    @P3A*/
                                   16616             +*/*     FIXED(15) - signed 2 byte - only allow a maximum value   @P3A*/
                                   16617             +*/*     of 32K.  There is a DFP PTM (KMM2552) for this problem.  @P3A*/

 003078 88F0 0001            00001 30283                       SRL   R15,1               In halfwords
 00307C 42F0 6303            00303 30284                       STC   R15,STOWLEN         Save for STOW
                                   30285              * the stow routine calls eov to allocate a new extent if
                                   30286              * the eob will not fit in the data set.  wylbur does not
                                   30287              * allow extra extents to be allocated and many times wylbur
                                   30288              * would abend x37 because no extent was defined or no extent
                                   30289              * would be available.  therefore, the following code is needed
                                   30290              * to determine if the eob will fit without calling eov.  it is
                                   30291              * a duplicate of the test made by r21 mvt stow module igg0210a.
                                   30292              *
                                   30293              * the code first checks if the eob will fit on the track being
                                   30294              * used.  if it won't then it uses the resident convert routines
                                   30295              * to determine if there is another track in the current extent.
                                   30296              * this is done by converting the current absolute address to
                                   30297              * ttrn form, add 1 track to the tt, and convert back to
                                   30298              * absolute form.  the convert back has a zero return code if
                                   30299              * the track is within the data set, or a four return code if not
                                   30300              *
                                   30301              * the resident routines use  r1 as the deb ptr, r2 as the
                                   30302              * absolute address area, r0 as the ttrn contents.  r1-r8 are
                                   30303              * not changed by the routines. par-r13 are changed. rar is the
                                   30304              * return register, and r15 is the entry address.

0                                  30970              *** ROUTINE TO WAIT FOR DISK I/O
                                   30971              ¿þþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþÜ
                                   30972              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   30973              Ÿ  UNDER NORMAL CIRCUMSTANCES, THIS ROUTINE GOES DIRECTLY TO THE      Ÿ
                                   30974              Ÿ    WYLBUR DISPATCHER.  THUS, THE REGISTERS ARE SAVED IN THE CP.     Ÿ
                                   30975              Ÿ    THE EXCEPTION TO THIS IS WHEN AN I/O OPERATION IS COMPLETED      Ÿ
                                   30976              Ÿ    IMMEDIATELY BECAUSE THERE IS NO MORE ROOM IN A PDS.  INSTEAD     Ÿ
                                   30977              Ÿ    OF LETTING THE CHECK MODULE CALL EOV AND ABEND, THE APPROPRIATE  Ÿ
                                   30978              Ÿ    FLAGS ARE TURNED OFF TO PREVENT STOW AND DSCB UPDATING AND       Ÿ
                                   30979              Ÿ    DCLOSE IS USED TO CLOSE THE DATA SET.  FOR THIS FUNCTION, IT     Ÿ
                                   30980              Ÿ    IS NECESSARY TO SAVE THE REGISTERS IN THE STANDARD WAY SO THAT   Ÿ
                                   30981              Ÿ    WHEN DCLOSE CALLS THE DISPATCHER THE REGISTERS IN THE CP ARE     Ÿ
                                   30982              Ÿ    NOT OVERLAID CAUSING A LOOP.                                     Ÿ
                                   30983              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
